### [236] [Random Access Expectation in DNA Storage and Fountain Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10919)
*Christoph Hofmeister,Rawad Bitar,Eitan Yaakobi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 针对DNA数据存储中的随机访问问题，研究了线性码的随机访问期望（即解码一个信息符号所需编码符号的期望数量），证明了二进制全对称码与LT码的等价性，并在大块长极限下分析出，采用剥解码器时归一化随机访问期望的下界为π/4≈0.7854，可实现值约为0.7869。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA数据存储中需要高效地从编码符号中解码出特定信息符号，即实现随机访问功能；已有工作推测全对称生成矩阵在最小化随机访问期望上具有最优性，但缺乏严格分析。

Method: 首先定义并形式化全对称码，指出其与LT码在二进制情形下的等价关系；随后在剥解码器（peeling decoder）和大块长极限假设下，对随机访问期望进行理论分析，推导其下界并给出可达构造。

Result: 二进制全对称码的归一化随机访问期望下界为π/4≈0.7854，且存在构造可实现约0.7869的值，两者非常接近。

Conclusion: 全对称码与LT码等价，其随机访问期望在渐近意义下接近π/4，该结果对DNA数据存储中编码方案的设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: Motivated by DNA data storage, we study the expected number of coded symbols drawn from a linear code until a desired information symbol can be decoded - the random access expectation. We focus on generator matrices with a type of symmetry, conjectured in prior work to be optimal, which we call fully symmetric. We point out an equivalence between binary fully symmetric codes and LT codes. Using this observation, we analyze the random access expectation of binary fully symmetric codes under a peeling decoder, in the large blocklength limit. Under these assumptions, the random access expectation, normalized by the number of information symbols, is at least π/4 {\approx} 0.7854, while a value of {\approx} 0.7869 is achievable.

</details>

### [237] [Representations of 3D Rotations: Mathematical Foundations and Comparative Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08086)
*Aizierjiang Aiersilan,Haochen Liu,James Hahn*

Main category: cs.GR

Method: 采用综合性文献调研方法，对欧拉角、轴角向量、四元数、旋转矩阵、指数映射以及新兴的连续和概率表示方法进行多维度对比分析，涵盖数学公式、连续性、万向锁敏感性、计算效率、存储需求、插值特性和复合运算等关键指标。

Result: 四元数在紧凑性和计算效率方面表现最优；6D连续表示和矩阵Fisher分布等替代方法在增强连续性和不确定性建模方面具有独特优势。

Conclusion: 未来研究方向可探索混合表示方法并开展全面的大规模评估，为旋转表示技术的改进奠定坚实基础。

Abstract: Rotation representations are foundational in fields such as computer graphics, robotics, and machine learning, where precise and efficient modeling of 3D orientations is critical. This paper comprehensively investigates diverse representations of the special orthogonal group $SO(3)$, such as Euler angles, axis-angle vectors, quaternions, rotation matrices, exponential maps, and emerging continuous and probabilistic methods, evaluating their mathematical formulations, continuity, susceptibility to gimbal lock, computational efficiency, storage requirements, interpolation properties, and composition operations, while integrating detailed algebraic insights with practical applications in fields like animation, pose estimation, inertial navigation, 3D shape registration, and neural networks. Empirical evidence highlights quaternions' dominance due to their compactness and computational efficiency, while alternatives like 6D continuous representations and matrix Fisher distributions provide enhanced continuity and uncertainty modeling. Future research could explore hybrid methods and thorough large-scale evaluations to help build a solid foundation for improving rotation representation techniques.

Abstract: We prove that a general planar NURBS curve parametrization $φ: [u_0,u_m] \xrightarrow{} C \subset \mathbb{R}^2$ admits an inverse map $φ^{-1}: C \xrightarrow{} [u_0,u_m]$ defined by rational splines. More specifically, we construct a family of rational spline functions on the curve $C$, present explicit formulas for their computation, and prove that the inverse parametrization admits a representation as a linear combination of these functions. Several examples are provided to illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach.

### [239] [Alice v1: Distillation-Enhanced Video Generation Surpassing Closed-Source Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08115)
*Wang Xiaoyu,Phong Nguyen,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: Alice v1是一个140亿参数的开源视频生成模型，通过带分数正则化的一致性蒸馏（rCM）方法，在仅需4步去噪（约8秒）的情况下，实现了比50步教师模型（Wan2.2）及其他闭源系统（Veo3、Sora2）更优的生成质量，VBench评分从84.0提升至91.2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 打破传统蒸馏以牺牲质量为代价换取速度的固有认知，探索能否通过蒸馏方法超越教师模型质量，同时实现显著加速。

Method: 采用带分数正则化的一致性蒸馏（rCM），包含三个关键机制：(1) 分数正则化项作为模式寻找目标，将概率质量集中在高质量输出上；(2) 针对教师模型处理不一致的失效模式（物理、手部、面部）构建带困难样本挖掘的合成数据流水线；(3) 一致性约束作为隐式正则化，消除对特定噪声样本的"幸运路径"依赖。

Result: Alice v1生成5秒720p 24fps视频仅需4步去噪（约8秒/H100），相比教师模型50步实现7倍加速；VBench评分从84.0提升至91.2，超越教师模型（Wan2.2）及闭源系统Veo3（~90）和Sora2（~88）；在人工偏好研究中表现具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 通过rCM蒸馏可以在加速推理的同时超越教师模型质量，为高效高质量视频生成提供了可行路径。项目全面开源以推动开放研究。

Abstract: Wepresent Alice v1, a 14-billion parameter open-source video generation model that achieves state-of-the-art quality through consistency distillation with score regularization (rCM). Contrary to conventional distillation-which trades quality for speed-we demonstrate that rCM-based distillation can exceed teacher model quality. We attribute this to three mechanisms: (1) the score regularization term acts as a mode-seeking objective that concentrates probability mass on high-quality outputs rather than covering the full teacher distribution, (2) our targeted synthetic data pipeline with hard example mining provides training signal specifically for failure modes (physics, hands, faces) that the teacher handles inconsistently, and (3) consistency enforcement acts as implicit regularization, eliminating "lucky path" dependence on specific noise samples. Alice v1 generates 5-second 720p videos at 24fps in 4 denoising steps (~8 seconds on H100), a 7x speedup over the 50-step teacher while improving VBench score from 84.0 (Wan2.2) to 91.2. This surpasses both the teacher and closed-source systems including Veo3 (~90) and Sora2 (~88) on automated benchmarks, with competitive results in human preference studies. We release all model weights, training code, synthetic data pipelines, and evaluation scripts to advance open research in video generation.

</details>


### [240] [MeshFIM: Local Low-Poly Mesh Editing via Fill-in-the-Middle Autoregressive Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08744)
*Dingdong Yang,Jian Liu,Biwen Lei,Haohan Weng,Zhuo Chen,Song Guo,Hao Richard Zhang,Ali Mahdavi Amiri,Chunchao Guo*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: MeshFIM提出了一种针对低多边形网格的填充式局部重建框架，通过五项设计解决边界附着、拓扑顺序和溢出控制等网格特有挑战，在交互编辑和缺陷修复任务中优于多种基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归模型生成低多边形网格时采用"全有或全无"方式，局部不满意时必须整体重新生成，造成计算浪费并破坏已有满意结构。亟需一种能够局部重建网格的方法。

Method: 提出MeshFIM框架，包含五项互补设计：边界顶点标记、上下文位置嵌入、扩展上下文宽度、上下文增强，以及采用门控减法机制的低多边形几何编码器，通过参考表面与现有网格的差异聚焦于缺失区域的生成。

Result: 在网格细化、网格修复以及整体生成+拼接方案上，MeshFIM优于多种基线方法；通过消融实验验证了每个组件的有效性。

Conclusion: MeshFIM实现了低多边形网格的局部重建，支持交互式笔刷编辑和自动缺陷修复两种应用，为网格生成任务提供了更高效的局部编辑范式。

Abstract: Autoregressive (AR) models can generate high-quality low-poly meshes from point clouds, but they still operate in an all-or-nothing manner: when a local region is unsatisfactory, the entire mesh must be regenerated, wasting computation and destroying satisfactory mesh structure elsewhere. We introduce MeshFIM, a Fill-in-the-Middle (FIM) framework that regenerates a target region of a low-poly mesh conditioned on the surrounding context. MeshFIM addresses three mesh-specific challenges: enforcing exact attachment along the exposed boundary, preserving topological order in the context, and suppressing overflow beyond the intended region. It does so with five complementary design choices: boundary vertex markers, context positional embeddings, expanded context width, context augmentation, and a low-poly geometry encoder whose gated subtraction mechanism focuses generation on the missing region by leveraging the difference between the reference surface and the existing mesh. Detailed ablation studies are presented to show the effectiveness of every introduced component. Based on MeshFIM, we demonstrate two applications: interactive brush-based editing and automatic defect repair on low-poly mesh (see Figure 1). Last but not least, experiments show that MeshFIM outperforms a range of baselines in mesh refinement, mesh repair and whole mesh generation plus stitch-back scheme.

</details>

Our method applies spatial decoupling across semantic scalp regions and structural decoupling along a hierarchical strand representation, progressing from global layout to fine-grained style. We further introduce a geometric tokenizer and region-aware semantic annotations to guide strand-level generation, enabling compositional editing, synthesis of rare and complex hairstyles, and adaptation to stylized domains. By aligning generative modeling with the workflow of digital grooming, HairGPT turns hair generation from opaque texture synthesis into a structured and semantically controllable authoring process, supporting robust semantic conditioning and high-fidelity results across realistic and stylized domains. Project Page: https://haiminluo.github.io/hairgpt/

*Ningxiao Tao,Baoquan Chen,Mengyu Chu*

Method: 将重建速度场参数化为连续的无散度核（Divergence-Free Kernel）表示，驱动拉格朗日3D高斯泼溅（3D Gaussian Splatting）表示的平流，内在保证流体的不可压缩性和长程传输相干性；引入滑动窗口（Sliding Window）方案在保持可负担训练成本的同时传播长时域梯度。

Conclusion: 通过结构性约束而非软惩罚的方式强制流体物理规律和传输一致性，结合无散度核与3D高斯泼溅表示及滑动窗口优化，有效解决了稀疏观测下3D流体重建的病态问题。

Abstract: Reconstructing 3D fluid velocity fields from sparse 2D video observations is a highly ill-posed inverse problem, demanding both transport consistency with observed motion and physical validity under fluid laws. Existing methods typically impose these constraints through soft penalties, often leading to compromised accuracy and convergence issues. We introduce a reconstruction framework that structurally enforces both constraints. Specifically, we parameterize the reconstructed velocity using a continuous Divergence-Free Kernel representation, driving the advection of a Lagrangian 3D Gaussian Splatting representation. This formulation intrinsically guarantees both flow incompressibility and long-range transport coherence by construction. To enable the efficient optimization of such a constrained system, we introduce a novel Sliding Window scheme that propagates gradients over meaningful temporal horizons while maintaining tractable training costs. Experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both transport consistency and physical accuracy, enabling applications such as high-quality re-simulation and flow analysis.

### [243] [FrameTwin: Curve-Anchored Gaussian Alignment from Sparse Views for Adaptive Wireframe 3D Printing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09362)
*Wenting Wang,Zhuo Huang,Kun Qian,Neelotpal Dutta,Yuhu Guo,Yingjun Tian,Yeung Yam,Charlie C. L. Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将高斯核锚定在参数化曲线上形成紧凑的几何感知编码，通过可微渲染管线估计神经变形场，对齐部分打印的目标模型与实际变形结构，利用变形场融合已打印畸变几何与未打印几何，自适应更新打印轨迹。

Abstract: We present FrameTwin, a curve-anchored Gaussian alignment framework that uses sparse-view images to close the control loop for adaptive wireframe 3D printing. Our key idea is to capture the deformation of thin wireframe structures from sparse-view images using Gaussian kernels anchored to parametric curves, yielding a compact and geometry-aware encoding that explicitly captures strut topology. Driven by a differentiable rendering pipeline, FrameTwin estimates a neural deformation field that aligns the partially printed target model with the deformed structure observed during fabrication, where the optimized curve-Gaussian representation serves as a digital twin of the evolving wireframe. Unlike general Gaussian-splatting approaches, our formulation constrains kernel placement along parametric curves, substantially reducing the ambiguity inherent in sparse-view observations of thin structures. The resultant deformation-field alignment enforces global consistency across all struts. By using the estimated deformation field to blend the distorted printed geometry with the remaining unprinted geometry, FrameTwin enables adaptive updates to future printing trajectories. We demonstrate that FrameTwin can robustly capture and compensate for deformation in wireframe models fabricated using a robotized 3D printing system.

### [244] [Geometrically Approximated Modeling for Emitter-Centric Ray-Triangle Filtering in Arbitrarily Dynamic LiDAR Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10457)
*Rabin Gajmer,Joonas Haapala,Zoltan Beck*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出Gajmer光线投射算法（GRCA），通过反转传统射线-三角形相交查询（从“每条射线击中什么”变为“每个三角形可能被哪些射线击中”），基于LiDAR发射器的旋转几何建模，实现无需加速结构的动态场景实时仿真，在复杂动态场景中相比OptiX和Embree分别获得最高7.97倍和14.55倍的加速，结合距离裁剪和混合管线可实现更大增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于加速结构（如BVH）的LiDAR仿真方法在处理大规模动态几何时，每帧需要重建加速结构，计算开销随场景动态程度线性增长且无法摊销，难以满足高分辨率多传感器实时仿真的需求。

Method: GRCA反转传统光线投射范式：将旋转式LiDAR发射器建模为旋转扫描的锥体或平面，对每个三角形计算其相对于发射器的表观面积，据此剔除无法被该三角形击中的通道和光线，无需任何加速结构。算法完全基于GPU计算且与厂商无关，可扩展至任意从已知原点发射光线的场景。

Result: 在2-8个128×4096线LiDAR（约100万条光线/帧）的复杂动态场景中：无距离裁剪时，GRCA达OptiX的7.97倍、Embree的14.55倍；加入10-100m距离裁剪后，在最复杂场景（约2200万三角形，900万动态，8个LiDAR）中达GPU 7.02倍、CPU 9.33倍；混合管线（GRCA处理动态+OptiX/Embree处理静态）达GPU 10.5倍、CPU 19.2倍。

Conclusion: GRCA通过反转射线-三角形相交查询范式，从根本上避免了动态场景中加速结构重建的开销，在高度动态、多传感器高分辨率LiDAR仿真场景中显著优于现有硬件加速方案，且该反转思路可推广至一般射线投射问题。

Abstract: Real-time Light Detection And Ranging (LiDAR) simulation must find, per emitted ray, the closest intersecting triangle even in dynamic scenes containing large numbers of moving and deformable objects. Dominant acceleration-structure approaches require rebuilding each frame for dynamic geometry -- a cost that compounds directly with scene dynamics and cannot be amortized regardless of how little actually changed.
  This paper presents the Gajmer Ray-Casting Algorithm (GRCA), which inverts the question: instead of asking what does each ray hit? it asks which rays can each triangle possibly hit? GRCA geometrically models spinning LiDAR emitters as rotation-traced cones or planes and uses each triangle's emitter-centric apparent area to cull, per triangle, which channels and the rays within those channels can possibly reach it -- without any acceleration structure. GRCA is compute-based and vendor-agnostic by design, targeting highly dynamic, high-resolution simultaneous multi-sensor simulation. At its core, GRCA is a general-purpose ray-casting algorithm: the emitter-centric inversion applies to any setting where rays originate from a known position, not only LiDAR.
  Benchmarks evaluate 2-8 simultaneous 128x4096-ray LiDARs (360deg/180deg) over complex dynamic scenes -- with just two sensors casting ~1M rays per frame. With range culling inactive, GRCA reaches up to 7.97x over hardware-accelerated OptiX (GPU) and 14.55x over Embree (CPU).
  Two independent extensions further boost performance even in the most complex scene (~22M triangles, ~9M of which are dynamic, 8 LiDARs): range culling at realistic deployment ranges (10-100m) reaches up to 7.02x GPU and 9.33x CPU; a hybrid pipeline -- GRCA for dynamic geometry, OptiX/Embree for static -- reaches up to 10.5x GPU and 19.2x CPU.

</details>

### [245] [CATO: Charted Attention for Neural PDE Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09016)
*Chun-Wun Cheng,Sifan Wang,Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb,Angelica I. Aviles-Rivero*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CATO是一种几何自适应且具有导数感知能力的神经算子，通过学习连续潜图表将网格坐标映射到学习到的图表空间，结合图表条件轴向注意力以降低计算成本，并引入导数感知物理损失以提高物理保真度，在多个数据集上实现了平均约26.76%的性能提升，同时参数量减少81.98%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的神经算子在处理复杂几何上的PDE时面临两大挑战：直接处理海量网格点计算成本过高，而在原始离散坐标上操作会掩盖内在几何结构，不利于物理交互的自然表达。

Method: CATO包含三个核心设计：(1) 学习连续潜图表（latent chart）将网格坐标映射到学习到的图表空间；(2) 图表条件轴向注意力（chart-conditioned axial attention）高效捕获长程依赖；(3) 导数感知物理损失（derivative-aware physics loss）联合监督解值、网格一致梯度及辅助通量场。

Result: 在所有评估数据集上取得最佳性能，相比最强基线平均提升约26.76%，同时参数量减少81.98%。

Conclusion: 学习几何自适应图表和导数感知物理监督能有效提升PDE算子学习的准确性与效率，且理论分析表明有利图表下图表轴向注意力能以可控误差表示低秩轴向解算子，图表微小扰动导致的近似退化有界。

Abstract: Neural operators have emerged as powerful data-driven solvers for PDEs, offering substantial acceleration over classical numerical methods. However, existing transformer-based operators still face critical challenges when modeling PDEs on complex geometries: directly processing over massive mesh points is computationally expensive, while operating in raw discretization coordinates may obscure the intrinsic geometry where physical interactions are more naturally expressed. To address these limitations, we introduce the Charted Axial Transformer Operator (CATO), a geometry-adaptive and derivative-aware neural operator for PDEs on general geometries. Instead of applying attention directly in the physical coordinate system, CATO learns a continuous latent chart that maps mesh coordinates into a learned chart space, where chart-conditioned axial attention efficiently captures long-range dependencies with reduced computational cost. In addition, CATO introduces a derivative-aware physics loss for steady-state PDEs that jointly supervises solution values, mesh-consistent gradients, and an auxiliary flux-like field, improving physical fidelity and reducing oversmoothing. We further provide a theoretical approximation result showing that, under a favorable chart, charted axial attention can represent low-rank axial solution operators with controlled error, and that small chart perturbations induce bounded approximation degradation. CATO achieves the best performance across all evaluated datasets, yielding an average improvement of approximately 26.76\% over the strongest competing baselines while reducing the number of parameters by 81.98\%. These results highlight the effectiveness of learning geometry-adaptive charts and derivative-aware physical supervision for accurate and efficient PDE operator learning.

</details>


### [246] [The Attacker in the Mirror: Breaking Self-Consistency in Safety via Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08427)
*Gabriele La Malfa,Emanuele La Malfa,Saar Cohen,Jie M. Zhang,Michael Luck,Michael Wooldridge,Elizabeth Black*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出锚定双策略自博弈（Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play），通过为攻击者和防御者训练独立的LoRA适配器（共享冻结基座模型），解决了传统自博弈中参数共享导致策略趋同、对抗压力消失的问题，在保持参数效率的同时显著提升安全鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自博弈红队方法中，攻击者和防御者共享同一模型参数，导致：(1) 纳什均衡解空间包含平凡拒答策略和预言机式防御者等不理想的广泛行为；(2) 参数联合更新使动力学坍缩为自一致性，攻击无法对防御者施加有效的对抗压力。

Method: 锚定双策略自博弈（ABSP）：在冻结的基座模型上训练角色特定的LoRA适配器，将攻击者和防御者的策略显式分离，同时通过共享基座模型保持优化稳定性。相比标准自博弈全参数微调，参数效率提升达100倍。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-{3B,7B,14B}-IT模型上，ABSP相比标准自博弈微调模型在安全基准上持续改进，且不损失推理能力。跨博弈实验表明，分离的攻击者和防御者模型在对抗防御和安全性上均优于自博弈方案。

Conclusion: 参数共享是自博弈红队的根本局限，显式角色分离的LoRA适配器策略既能维持对抗压力，又能保证训练稳定，为AI安全对齐提供了更高效、更鲁棒的范式。

Abstract: Self-play red team is an established approach to improving AI safety in which different instances of the same model play attacker and defender roles in a zero-sum game, i.e., where the attacker tries to jailbreak the defender; if self-play converges to a Nash equilibrium, the model is guaranteed to respond safely within the settings of the game. Although the parameter sharing enforced by the use of the same model for the two roles improves stability and performance, it introduces fundamental theoretical and architectural limitations. We show that the set of Nash equilibria that can be reached corresponds to a broad class of behaviours that includes trivial always refuse strategies and oracle-like defenders, thus limiting practical applicability. We then show that when attacker and defender share and update the same base model, the dynamics collapse to self-consistency, so that attacks do not enforce adversarial pressure on the defender. In response, we propose Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play, which trains distinct role-specific LoRA adapters on top of a frozen base model, thereby maintaining stable optimisation while preserving adversarial pressure through explicit role separation. In relation to standard self-play, we show up to 100x greater parameter efficiency than finetuning and consistent improvements in safety compared to self-play fine-tuned models. We evaluate on Qwen2.5-{3B, 7B,14B}-IT models across widely used safety benchmarks, showing improved robustness without loss of reasoning ability. Cross-play experiments further show that our attacker and defender models are superior to self-play in terms of adversarial defence and safety.

</details>


### [247] [Automated Approach for Solving Infinite-state Polynomial Reachability Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10169)
*Krishnendu Chatterjee,Ehsan Kafshdar Goharshady,Mehrdad Karrabi,Maximilian Seeliger,Đorđe Žikelić*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对无限状态图上的回合制可达性游戏，提出了排名证书（ranking certificates）作为证明REACH玩家存在获胜策略的完备推理规则，并针对多项式约束描述的多项式可达性游戏设计了全自动算法，能够计算获胜策略并生成形式化正确性证明。该算法是可靠、半完备的，运行时间为次指数级，在经典Cinderella-Stepmother游戏中首次实现了任意精度参数下的最优获胜策略计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可达性游戏在人工智能和响应式合成中有重要应用，许多实际场景涉及无限状态图。现有方法难以处理此类无限状态可达性游戏，因此需要新的理论框架和自动化算法。

Method: (1) 提出排名证书（ranking certificates）作为可达性游戏的形式化证明规则，完备且可靠；(2) 针对多项式可达性游戏（转移和目标由实变量上的多项式约束描述），设计全自动算法以同时计算获胜策略和排名证书形式的正确性证明，算法运行在次指数时间。

Result: 算法是可靠（sound）、半完备（semi-complete）的，能解决现有方法无法处理的挑战性实例；在经典Cinderella-Stepmother游戏中首次实现任意精度参数下的最优获胜策略计算。

Conclusion: 所提的排名证书为无限状态可达性游戏提供了坚实的理论基础，自动化算法填补了该领域在实践求解上的空白，展现了优于现有方法的求解能力。

Abstract: Reachability games are two-player games played on a graph, where the objective of $\texttt{REACH}$ player is to reach the target set whereas the objective of $\texttt{SAFE}$ player is to stay away from the target set. Reachability games have important applications in artificial intelligence and reactive synthesis, and many of these applications give rise to infinite-state reachability games. In this paper, we study turn-based reachability games on infinite-state graphs defined over valuations of a finite set of real variables. We consider the problem of determining the existence of and computing a winning strategy for $\texttt{REACH}$ player. Our contributions are twofold. First, we propose ranking certificates for reachability games, a sound and complete proof rule for proving that $\texttt{REACH}$ player has a winning strategy from the specified initial state. Second, we consider polynomial reachability games, where transitions and objectives are described by polynomial constraints over real variables, and propose a fully automated algorithm for computing a winning strategy for $\texttt{REACH}$ player together with a formal correctness witness in the form of a ranking certificate. The algorithm is sound, semi-complete, and runs in sub-exponential time. Our experiments demonstrate the ability of our method to solve challenging examples from the literature that were out of the reach of existing methods. Specifically, for the classical Cinderella-Stepmother game, we are able to compute an optimal winning strategy for an arbitrary precision parameter for the first time.

</details>


### [248] [Fairness of Explanations in Artificial Intelligence (AI): A Unifying Framework, Axioms, and Future Direction toward Responsible AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09852)
*Gideon Popoola,John Sheppard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该综述识别了算法公平性与可解释AI（XAI）交叉领域中的盲点——即使模型输出满足所有标准公平性指标，其推理过程仍可能存在严重偏差（即程序性偏差）。论文提出了一个条件不变性框架来形式化解释公平性，要求解释在给定任务相关特征时与受保护属性无关；引入七维分类法，识别了解释不平等的三种生成机制，并给出了六步评估工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有算法公平性和可解释AI（XAI）研究相对独立，忽略了一个关键盲点：模型输出可以满足所有公平性标准，但其内部推理过程（即解释）可能仍存在深刻的不公平性。作者称之为"程序性偏差"，并指出需要将解释的公平性作为一个独立的科学研究对象。

Method: 采用统一的理论与文献综述方法，提出了条件不变性框架形式化解释公平性，引入七维分类法，识别三种生成机制（表示驱动、解释模型不匹配、可操作性驱动），并给出六步评估工作流。

Result: 首次对解释公平性这一新兴领域进行了统一的理论与文献综述；指出现有后验解释器在认证解释公平性方面的缺陷；提出的条件不变性框架可以统一现有所有解释公平性指标作为其部分实现。

Conclusion: 解释公平性是一个独立且重要的研究方向，不能仅通过输出公平性来保证；条件不变性框架为解释公平性提供了统一的理论基础，七维分类法和六步工作流为实践中的解释公平性审计提供了可操作指南。

Abstract: Machine learning algorithms are being used in high-stakes decisions, including those in criminal justice, healthcare, credit, and employment. The research community has responded with two largely independent research fields: \emph{algorithmic fairness}, which targets equitable outcomes, and \emph{explainable AI} (XAI), which targets interpretable reasoning. This survey identifies and maps a novel blind spot at their intersection, which is a model that can satisfy every standard fairness criterion in its outputs while being profoundly unfair in its \emph{reasoning process}. We refer to this as the procedural bias, and mitigating it requires treating the fairness of explanations as a distinct object of scientific study.
  To our knowledge, we provide the first unified theoretical and literature review of this emerging field and elucidate the drawbacks of post-hoc explainers in certifying explanation fairness. Our central contribution is a \emph{conditional invariance framework} formalizing explanation fairness as the requirement that explanations should be indifferent regardless of the protected attributes $ P(E(X) \in \cdot \mid X_\text{rel} = x_\text{rel},\, A = a) = P(E(X) \in \cdot \mid X_\text{rel} = x_\text{rel},\, A = b)$ for all task-relevant $x$, a single principle from which all existing explanation fairness metrics emerge as partial operationalizations. We introduce a seven-dimensional taxonomy, identify three generative mechanisms of explanation inequity (representation-driven, explanation-model mismatch, actionability-driven), and propose a canonical six-step evaluation workflow for operationalizing explanation fairness audits in practice.

</details>

### [249] [Mechanism Design Is Not Enough: Prosocial Agents for Cooperative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08426)
*Xuanqiang Angelo Huang,Charlie Tharas,Samuele Marro,Van Q. Truong,Bernhard Schölkopf,Emanuele La Malfa,Zhijing Jin*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文证明，仅靠机制设计（不完全合同理论）不足以最大化LLM智能体的社会福利，存在无法消除的福利损失；而亲社会智能体（兼顾他人利益）可以弥补这一差距，实现更优的社会和个体结果。实验表明，在多智能体资源分配和社会困境中，亲社会性是有益的。对AI安全的启示：仅设计充分机制不够，智能体必须被构建为具有内在亲社会性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保AI智能体在与其他主体互动时安全且有益地行为，是当代AI安全的核心挑战之一。机制设计虽能激励合作行为，但尚不清楚仅靠它是否足以最大化LLM智能体的社会福利。

Method: 借鉴不完全合同理论，形式化证明当合同无法区分所有相关未来偶发事件时，存在任何现实机制都无法消除的严格正福利损失；并通过多智能体资源分配环境与经典社会困境实验，验证亲社会智能体的效果。

Result: 证明存在不可消除的福利损失缺口，亲社会智能体能关闭这一缺口，实现社会更优且个体有利的结果；实验证实LLM驱动的智能体中亲社会性有益。

Conclusion: 对AI安全的启示：设计充分的机制并不足够，必须构建具有内在亲社会性的智能体，才能实现大规模合作互动。

Abstract: Ensuring that AI agents behave safely and beneficially when interacting with other parties has emerged as one of the central challenges of modern AI safety. While mechanism design, as the theory of designing rules to align individual and collective objectives, can incentivize cooperative behavior, it is still an open question whether it alone is sufficient to maximize LLM agents' social welfare. This work proves that the answer is negative: drawing from incomplete contract theory, we formally show that when contracts cannot distinguish all relevant future contingencies, there is a strictly positive welfare loss that no realistic mechanism can eliminate. We show that prosocial agents, who weigh others' welfare alongside their own, can close this gap and achieve outcomes that are socially superior and individually beneficial. Experimentally, we show that in multi-agent resource-allocation environments and canonical social dilemmas where agents are powered by large language models, prosociality is beneficial. The implication for AI safety is clear: to enable cooperative interactions at scale, designing adequate mechanisms is not sufficient; agents must be built to be intrinsically prosocial.

### [250] [On MMS, APS and XOS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08859)
*Uriel Feige,Vadim Grinberg*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究XOS估值下不可分物品的公平分配问题，通过分析APS与MMS之间的差距，设计了分配算法，首次实现优于1/4的MMS近似比（11/40），并在足够大n时成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前工作只能达到从下方趋近1/4的MMS近似比（当前最优为4/17），本文旨在突破1/4这一阈值，获得更好的近似比。

Method: 首先研究所有agent具有相同XOS估值时APS与MMS的差距，设计分配算法证明每个agent获得至少11/40倍APS；然后从该算法获得灵感，修改后适用于不同XOS估值的情形，并证明存在足够大的n_0使得对所有n≥n_0上述结果成立。

Result: 对于足够大的n，实现了α > 11/40的MMS（及APS）分配，突破了此前1/4的障碍。

Conclusion: 通过分析APS与MMS的差距并设计相应算法，在XOS估值下实现了优于1/4的MMS近似比，但该结果仅在agent数量足够大时成立。

Abstract: We consider allocations of a set of $m$ indivisible goods to $n$ agents of equal entitlements that have valuations from the class XOS. A previous sequence of works showed allocations that obtain an $α$-approximation for the maximin share (MMS), for values of $α$ that gradually approach $\frac{1}{4}$ from below (the currently known ratio is $\frac{4}{17}$). In this work we attempt to obtain ratios better than $\frac{1}{4}$, and manage to do so for sufficiently large $n$. Our methodology is to first investigate the gap between the anyprice share (APS) and the MMS when all agents have the same XOS valuations, for which we design an allocation algorithm and prove that each agent receives at least $α> \frac{11}{40}$ times the APS. Then, we derive inspiration from this algorithm, and modify it so that it applies also when agents have different XOS valuations. Using this modified version, we show that for some sufficiently large $n_0$, there is an $α$-MMS allocation (in fact, an $α$-APS allocation) for every $n \geq n_0$.

### [251] [Pacing Equilibria in Second-Price Auctions with Few Goods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09332)
*Yiyang Huang,Yonglei Yan,Zihe Wang,Zhengyang Liu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了在在线广告拍卖中计算第二价格计调均衡（SPPE）的多项式时间算法：对于常数商品数量，通过将出价乘数映射到最高出价来划分参数空间为几何单元，枚举单元后转化为线性可行性问题；该可解性可扩展到任意商品数量但估值类型为常数的大规模市场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SPPE是在线广告拍卖中的基础模型，但其计算复杂度尚未被充分解决，需要有效的算法来精确计算均衡。

Method: 将买家的计调乘数映射到每种商品上的最高出价，将参数空间划分为不同的几何单元；通过枚举这些单元固定出价的相对顺序，将均衡计算问题简化为线性可行性程序。

Result: 对于常数商品数量的实例，提出了多项式时间精确SPPE算法；并证明当商品可聚合成常数种估值类型时，该可解性可推广到任意商品数量的大规模市场。

Conclusion: SPPE在常数商品或常数估值类型下是多项式时间可解的，为在线广告拍卖中的均衡计算提供了理论基础和实用算法。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the computation of second-price pacing equilibria (SPPEs), a foundational model in online advertising auctions. We present a polynomial-time algorithm for computing exact SPPEs in instances with a constant number of goods. Our core technique maps buyers' pacing multipliers to the highest bids on each good, effectively partitioning the parameter space into a set of distinct geometric cells. By enumerating these cells, we fix the relative ordering of the bids and reduce the problem of equilibrium computation to a linear feasibility program. Finally, we demonstrate that this tractability extends to large-scale markets with an arbitrary number of goods, provided the goods can be aggregated into a constant number of valuation types.

</details>


### [252] [Efficient Ensemble Selection from Binary and Pairwise Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09588)
*Tzeh Yuan Neoh,Nicholas Teh,Je Qin Chooi,Paul W. Goldberg,Milind Tambe*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了组织在多个AI系统中选择小型高性能集成委员会的问题，将其建模为分布化多赢家投票问题。在二值反馈设置下，提出失败条件化贪心算法，在保持(1-1/e)保证的同时获得实例依赖的查询节省。在成对反馈设置下，证明了全信息优化具有PTAS但无EPTAS，目标函数单调但不子模，并提出加权序数覆盖松弛方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Organizations increasingly deploy multiple AI systems across task domains, but selecting a small, high-performing ensemble can require costly model calls, benchmark runs, and human evaluation. We study this selection problem as a distributional variant of multiwinner voting: tasks are drawn from an unknown domain distribution, each task induces feedback over candidate experts, and a committee's value on a task is determined by its best-performing member. We analyze both binary feedback, for tasks with correct/incorrect outcomes, and pairwise feedback, for tasks where candidate outputs are compared by preference. In the binary setting, the induced objective is coverage. We give exhaustive-elicitation baselines and matching worst-case query lower bounds, and we design a failure-conditioned greedy algorithm that preserves the standard $(1-1/e)$ guarantee while obtaining instance-dependent query savings. In the pairwise setting, we study $θ$-winning committees. We show that full-information optimization admits a PTAS but no EPTAS under Gap-ETH, and that the objective is monotone but not submodular. This motivates a weighted ordinal coverage relaxation, which is submodular and supports a failure-conditioned greedy oracle under pairwise feedback. We then convert this oracle back into $θ$-type guarantees through finite-family auditing or a minimax wrapper. We also provide small-scale LLM experiments illustrating the predicted query savings and the role of complementarity in committee selection.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Prediction markets rely on liquidity to convert trades into informative prices, yet existing mechanisms fix liquidity ex ante. This restriction enforces a static trade-off between price responsiveness and worst-case loss despite inherently nonstationary trading conditions. We propose a fundamentally different approach that treats liquidity selection itself as an online learning problem. Our mechanism mixes a family of cost-function markets via learnable weights, yielding a single adaptive market that preserves no-arbitrage, bounded worst-case loss, expressiveness, and positive upside. We introduce a hybrid structural risk signal, a per-round objective that quantifies the trade-off between price impact and inventory risk, and show that standard online learning algorithms achieve switching-regret guarantees relative to the best sequence of liquidity regimes in hindsight. Simulations demonstrate that the mechanism adaptively shifts liquidity across regimes in response to both order flow and inventory dynamics. Our results establish a principled framework for adaptive liquidity, connecting prediction market design with online learning.

### [254] [Structure from Strategic Interaction & Uncertainty Risk Sensitive Games for Robust Preference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09946)
*Max Horwitz,Jake Gonzales,Eric Mazumdar,Lillian J. Ratliff*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出风险敏感偏好博弈，将大语言模型的偏好微调从风险中性纳什学习扩展为考虑尾部风险的凸风险度量优化，通过保持单调性实现高效自对弈收敛，并引入分层博弈与双时间尺度外梯度算法消除偏差，实验证明该方法在不牺牲平均性能的前提下提升了跨数据层的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于纳什学习的偏好微调方法（NLHF）只优化期望成对收益，导致具有相似胜率但尾部行为不同的策略被混为一谈，模型可能在部分提示、标注者或关键安全层面上系统性失败，缺乏对分布中不同区域的风险控制能力。

Method: 1) 将偏好微调建模为风险敏感偏好博弈，使用凸风险度量替代期望损失，利用风险度量的平移不变性保持优化单调性；2) 建立分层博弈（hierarchical game）与双时间尺度外梯度算法，结合偏差校正，实现Stackelberg均衡收敛；3) 给出离线样本复杂度界限，同时控制非线性风险变换的结构偏差、风险估计的统计偏差以及风险敏感设置下的浓度行为。

Result: 风险调整后的策略在各数据层（strata）上表现出鲁棒性，在不同风险选择下保持稳定，性能持平或超越风险中性基线，实现了无需性能代价的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 风险敏感偏好博弈有效解决了NLHF中平均表现掩盖尾部失败的问题，通过理论保证和实证验证表明，该方法能在不牺牲平均性能的前提下显著提升模型在分布各层级的鲁棒性，为安全关键的偏好微调提供了新范式。

Abstract: A growing line of work reframes preference-based fine-tuning of large language models game-theoretically: Nash Learning from Human Feedback (NLHF) recasts the problem as a zero-sum game over policies. However, optimization is over expected pairwise payoffs, thereby conflating policies with similar win rates but different tail behavior. As such, these methods are agnostic to where in the data distribution they succeed or fail: strong average performance can mask systematic failure across prompts, annotators, or safety-critical strata. We introduce risk-sensitive preference games, in which players optimize convex risk measures of their preference loss, exploiting structure in preference uncertainty. While risk-sensitivity generally breaks the zero-sum structure, we show that translation invariance of many risk metrics ensures that we retain monotonicity, yielding fast convergence of sample-efficient self-play methods. Furthermore, we establish algorithmic stability and offline sample complexity bounds that scale with risk, requiring simultaneous control of structural bias from nonlinear risk transformations, statistical bias in risk estimation, and concentration tailored to the risk-sensitive setting. To address statistical bias, we introduce a hierarchical game formulation and a two-timescale extragradient algorithm with bias correction that converges to the Stackelberg equilibrium and is especially effective in low-sample regimes. Empirically, risk-adjusted policies are robust across data strata, stable across risk choices, and match or exceed risk-neutral performance thereby achieving robustness without a performance tax.

</details>


### [255] [A Resource Allocation Game and its Equilibrium Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09988)
*Duan-Shin Lee*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出一个贝叶斯博弈模型来分配资源，分析了两人博弈中交替恒等-平坦（AIF）策略函数的纳什均衡，并针对大规模n人博弈给出了平均场一阶近似和高斯二阶近似，提出了一种构造算法，该算法能在有限步内收敛到纳什均衡，并在梯度冲突条件下产生一个连续严格递增的“颤振”策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 资源分配问题中，玩家对资源有异质需求且策略交互复杂，传统方法难以刻画均衡行为，需要一种博弈论框架来分析玩家策略并找到均衡解。

Method: 建立贝叶斯博弈模型，采用最小请求优先且全有或全无的分配规则；对两人博弈，在AIF函数族内解析分析均衡策略；对大规模n人博弈，利用平均场理论给出O(n)阶资源下的一阶近似和二阶高斯近似，并设计一种有限步收敛的构造算法处理梯度冲突导致的颤振现象。

Result: 两人博弈中纳什均衡由两个恒等函数、具有公共切换点的两个AIF函数、或分别具有1个和3个切换点的两个AIF函数构成；大规模游戏中一阶分析得到单切换点AIF均衡；构造算法可处理颤振并保证有限步终止。

Conclusion: 该贝叶斯博弈框架和构造算法为资源分配问题提供了一种新的均衡分析工具，尤其在大型游戏中能有效处理策略复杂性并保证均衡存在性。

Abstract: In this paper we propose a Bayesian game to allocate resources.
  In this game, there are $c$ units of resources to be
  allocated to $n$ players. Agent $i$ has a demand of $V_i$ units of resources
  and takes action $X_i$ according to a strategy function $s_i$, \ie $X_i=s_i(V_i)$.
  Payoffs are setup such that player $i$ is contented with no more than $V_i$
  units of resources. We assume that resources are granted to the players
  on a smallest-request-first and all-or-nothing basis.
  For this game with two players, we analyze the equilibrium strategy
  functions mathematically within the family of alternating identity-and-flat (AIF)
  functions. We show that Nash equilibrium profiles consist of two identity functions,
  two AIF functions with a common switch point, or two AIF functions with one
  and three switch points, respectively.
  For an $n$-player game with a large $n$ and a large $c_n$
  of order $O(n)$, we present a mean-field first order approximation and a
  second-order Gaussian approximation for its
  equilibrium strategy function. The first-order analysis obtains an equilibrium
  AIF function with one switch point. In Gaussian analysis of large games, we
  propose a construction algorithm. This construction algorithm begins in searching
  within the family of AIF functions. If a gradient conflict condition occurs, the game
  enters a chattering regime, in which players
  play a continuous, strictly increasing strategy function that is not an identity nor a flat function.
  Conceptually one can view the chattering regime as if players alternate between
  a slope-one strategy and a flat strategy infinitely fast in order to sustain a high payoff.
  We prove that the construction algorithm always
  obtains a Nash equilibrium and terminates in a finite number of steps.
  We present several numerical examples for the two player game as well as the Gaussian model.

</details>


### [256] [The Vote-Left Equilibrium: A Deterministic Coordination Strategy for the Faithful in The Traitors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10233)
*Vince Knight*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出Vote-Left协议，一种确定性投票规则，使每个存活玩家在固定循环顺序中投票给下一个存活者。在完全遵守下，放逐分布与随机投票相同，但由于投票是公开信息的确定性函数，任何偏离都可被立即识别。结合简单惩罚规则，Vote-Left在nt > 2mt + 2条件下构成完美贝叶斯均衡（涵盖所有电视播放配置），并在晚期阶段（nt ≤ 2mt + 2）刻画了叛徒的最佳应对。在电视播放配置中，Vote-Left将忠诚信徒的获胜概率提高了约三倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交推理游戏中，随机投票对不知情多数（Faithful）在同时信号协议下是最优的，但个体投票时随机投票无法与策略性投票区分，Faithful仍暴露于叛徒（Traitor）的协调勾结之下。现有方法无法有效解决这一问题。

Method: 提出Vote-Left协议，一种基于固定循环顺序的确定性投票规则。该协议使每个玩家投票给下一个存活者，投票行为是公开信息的确定性函数，任何偏离可被立即检测。结合一个简单的惩罚规则，确保协议在特定条件下构成完美贝叶斯均衡。

Result: Vote-Left在nt > 2mt + 2条件下构成完美贝叶斯均衡（涵盖所有电视播放配置）。刻画了晚期阶段（nt ≤ 2mt + 2）叛徒的最佳应对策略。在电视播放配置中，Faithful的获胜概率相比随机投票提高了约三倍。

Conclusion: Vote-Left协议通过确定性投票规则和可检测的偏离机制，有效提升了社交推理游戏中不知情多数（Faithful）的获胜概率，尤其在电视播放的配置下效果显著。

Abstract: The Traitors is a social deduction game in which an informed minority of Traitors face an uninformed majority of Faithful, and the
  recurring question facing the Faithful is how to vote. Random voting is known to be optimal for the uninformed majority under
  simultaneous-signal protocols [Braverman, Etesami and Mossel, 2008], but when votes are cast individually, random votes are
  indistinguishable from strategic ones and the Faithful remain exposed to coordinated Traitor collusion. We introduce the Vote-Left
  protocol, a deterministic rule under which every player votes for the next surviving player in a fixed cyclic ordering. Under full
  compliance every surviving player receives exactly one vote, so the banishment distribution coincides with random voting; since
  prescribed votes are deterministic functions of public information, any deviation is immediately identifiable. Combined with a simple
  punishment rule, Vote-Left constitutes a Perfect Bayesian Equilibrium for every state with $n_t > 2m_t + 2$, a region that contains every
  televised configuration. We characterise the Traitors' best response in the late-game phase ($n_t \leq 2m_t + 2$): deviate via collusion
  once the Faithful no longer have enough votes to guarantee punishment. Across the configurations played on television, Vote-Left raises
  the Faithful's winning probability by a factor of approximately three over random voting under collusion.

</details>


### [257] [Regret Minimization in Bilateral Trade With Perturbed Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10475)
*Anna Lunghi,Matteo Castiglioni,Alberto Marchesi*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究重复交易中在全局预算平衡约束下最大化交易收益（GFT）的问题。通过研究受扰动的市场（随机分布受到对抗性污染C），设计了一种自适应算法，实现了对最佳预算平衡价格分布的$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4}) + \mathcal{O}(C\log(T))$遗憾界，同时在完全对抗环境下保持$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4})$的遗憾界，弥合了对抗环境与随机环境之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在重复买卖双方交易中最大化交易收益（GFT）问题，在纯对抗和纯随机环境下存在显著二分法：对抗环境只能学习固定价格机制，而随机环境可学习期望预算平衡的价格分布，后者可使GFT提升两倍。现有研究无法弥合这一差距，因此需要在介于两者之间的扰动市场中寻找自适应算法。

Method: 研究扰动市场模型，其中底层为随机分布但受到幅度为C的对抗性污染。设计了一种自适应算法，该算法能够根据污染程度C动态调整，在随机性占主导时逼近随机环境最优性能，在对抗性占主导时退化为鲁棒的对抗环境保障。

Result: 算法实现了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4}) + \mathcal{O}(C\log(T))$的遗憾界（针对最佳预算平衡价格分布），同时在完全对抗环境下保持$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4})$的遗憾界（针对每轮预算平衡基线），实现了最优性。

Conclusion: 通过扰动市场模型成功弥合了对抗与随机环境之间的GFT最大化差距，证明了算法能自适应地随污染程度缩放，在两种极端环境之间实现平滑过渡和最优保障。

Abstract: We address the problem of maximizing Gain from Trade (GFT) in repeated buyer-seller exchanges subject to global budget balance constraints. While this problem is well-understood in purely adversarial and stochastic settings, these environments exhibit a sharp dichotomy: adversarial environments allow for no-regret learning against the best fixed-price mechanism, whereas stochastic environments allow for no-regret learning against the best distribution over prices that is budget balanced in expectation. This gap is significant, as policies balanced in expectation can increase the GFT by a multiplicative factor of two. In this work, we bridge these extremes by studying perturbed markets, where an underlying stochastic distribution is subject to an adversarial corruption $C$. We design an algorithm that adaptively scales with the level of corruption, achieving an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4}) + \mathcal{O}(C\log(T))$ regret bound against the best budget-balanced distribution over prices. Simultaneously, our algorithm maintains the worst-case $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{3/4})$ regret bound relative to a per-round budget-balanced baseline, ensuring optimality even in fully adversarial environments.

</details>


### [258] [Online Resource Allocation With General Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10519)
*Eleonora Fidelia Chiefari,Francesco Emanuele Stradi,Matteo Castiglioni,Alberto Marchesi*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究包含预算约束和一般约束的在线资源分配问题，提出一种算法在随机和对抗两种环境下均达到最佳保证，同时严格满足预算约束并实现一般约束的累积违规为Õ(√T)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典在线资源分配仅考虑预算约束，无法建模实际应用中的关键经济约束（如ROI约束），因此需要将框架扩展到包含一般约束的场景。

Method: 提出一种新算法，利用弱自适应性（weak adaptivity）分析来保证拉格朗日乘子的有界性，从而克服一般约束与预算约束对齐性差的难题，实现在随机和对抗两种机制下的最佳保证。

Result: 在随机机制下对动态基准达到Õ(√T)遗憾，在对抗机制下达到Õ(√T)的α-遗憾（α取决于离线问题的可行性裕度）；严格满足预算约束，一般约束的累积违规为Õ(√T)。

Conclusion: 该工作将在线资源分配从纯预算约束推广到包含一般约束的更广泛场景，技术上揭示了弱自适应性在解决约束对齐问题中的关键作用。

Abstract: Online resource allocation (ORA) is a fundamental framework for sequential decision-making problems under budget constraints, with applications ranging from online advertising to revenue management. In this work, we study a broader setting that includes both budget constraints and general constraints, extending the classical budget-only model. This extension is essential for modeling critical economic requirements, such as Return-on-Investment (ROI) constraints. We develop an algorithm that achieves best-of-both-world guarantees within this generalized framework. In particular, against a dynamic benchmark, our algorithm achieves $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret in the \emph{stochastic} regime and $α$-regret of order $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(\sqrt{T})$ in the \emph{adversarial} regime, where $α$ depends on the feasibility margin of the corresponding offline problem. At the same time, our algorithm guarantees strict satisfaction of the budget constraints and $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(\sqrt{T})$ cumulative violation for the general ones. From a technical perspective, introducing general constraints alongside budgets precludes the use of standard budget-focus methods. While budget methods rely on a zero-consumption ``safe'' action to ensure feasibility, general constraints are much less ``aligned'' towards feasibility. We overcome these difficulties with a new analysis that exploits \emph{weak adaptivity} to get boundedness of the Lagrangian multipliers and best-of-both-world guarantees.

### [259] [Constant Inapproximability for Fisher Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10802)
*Argyrios Deligkas,John Fearnley,Alexandros Hollender,Themistoklis Melissourgos*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了Fisher市场中可分离分段线性凹（SPLC）效用函数下近似市场均衡的计算问题，证明常数近似比（优于1/11）是PPAD完全的，从而排除了PTAS存在的可能性（除非PPAD=P），并将此不可近似性结果推广至Arrow-Debreu交换市场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前仅知SPLC效用函数的Fisher市场均衡在逆多项式近似下是PPAD完全的，但常数近似下的复杂性未知。本文旨在探究是否存在常数近似比的多项式时间算法，从而划清该问题的计算边界。

Method: 通过构造从已知PPAD完全问题到SPLC Fisher市场均衡近似问题的归约，设计精巧的效用函数和初始禀赋，使得任意优于1/11近似比的算法均可用于求解源问题，从而证明PPAD完全性。

Result: 证明了计算任何优于1/11近似比的SPLC Fisher市场均衡是PPAD完全的，意味着不存在PTAS（除非PPAD=P），并将该不可近似性界推广至Arrow-Debreu交换市场。

Conclusion: SPLC效用函数下的Fisher市场均衡近似问题具有常数近似下界的不可近似性，1/11是一个硬阈值，进一步刻画了该问题的计算复杂度本质。

Abstract: We study the problem of computing approximate market equilibria in Fisher markets with separable piecewise-linear concave (SPLC) utility functions. In this setting, the problem was only known to be PPAD-complete for inverse-polynomial approximations. We strengthen this result by showing PPAD-hardness for constant approximations. This means that the problem does not admit a polynomial time approximation scheme (PTAS) unless PPAD$=$P. In fact, we prove that computing any approximation better than $1/11$ is PPAD-complete. As a direct byproduct of our main result, we get the same inapproximability bound for Arrow-Debreu exchange markets with SPLC utility functions.

</details>

### [260] [Diffusion Restore: Real-Time Markov Chain Monte Carlo Light Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08916)
*Sascha Holl,Gurprit Singh,Hans-Peter Seidel*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: Diffusion Restore 是一个基于扩散模型的 MCMC 光传输实时框架，通过选择无需 Metropolis 调整的非可逆扩散局部动力学，在局部探索中引入动量以实现更定向的探索，在理论保证下达到了新的 SOTA 性能，并在 GPU 上实现了实时光线追踪帧率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCMC 光传输方法中，控制目标分布的探索仍然具有挑战性——需要平衡局部探索与全局发现，且局部动力学必须快速探索单个模态而不陷入停滞或过度回溯。全局发现问题已由 Restore 框架解决，但局部探索效率仍有待提升。

Method: 基于 Restore 框架，选择扩散模型作为局部动力学，完全避免 Metropolis 调整（已知会减慢收敛速度）；将动力学建模为非可逆过程，在漂移中引入动量，实现比可逆随机游走更定向的探索；同时提供了理论正确性证明。

Result: 在多种场景下，Diffusion Restore 超越了所有现有的 MCMC 光传输方法，建立了新的 SOTA；在实时渲染设置中（如交互应用和游戏）也优于传统的 Path Tracing 方法；通过光线追踪和计算着色器的 GPU 实现达到了实时的帧率。

Conclusion: 提出的 Diffusion Restore 不仅在离线渲染中表现优越，在实时渲染中同样超越了传统路径追踪方法，证明了其作为实时 MCMC 光传输框架的有效性和实用性。

Abstract: We present Diffusion Restore, a real-time framework for diffusion-based MCMC light transport. MCMC methods are highly suitable for sampling from complex high-dimensional distributions and for approximating integrals over them. In practice, they are often the only viable solution when direct sampling is not possible and alternative methods are either inefficient or cannot be applied due to the structure of the target distribution. However, controlling the exploration of the target distribution in MCMC methods remains challenging. Efficient exploration requires a balance between local exploration and global discovery, and local dynamics must rapidly explore individual modes without getting stuck or exhibiting excessive backtracking. The problem of global discovery has recently been addressed by the introduction of the Restore framework. In this work, we build on this framework and focus on improving local exploration. We show how to choose diffusion-based local dynamics within the Restore framework while completely avoiding Metropolis-adjustment, which is known to slow down convergence. Furthermore, we model these dynamics as nonreversible, introducing momentum in the drift and thereby enabling more directed exploration of the target distribution compared to reversible, random-walk-like dynamics. We provide a theoretical justification for the validity of our choice of local dynamics. Empirically, we demonstrate across diverse scenes that Diffusion Restore outperforms all existing MCMC light transport methods and establishes a new state of the art. In addition, we present a GPU implementation in ray tracing and compute shaders and achieve real-time frame rates. This demonstrates that Diffusion Restore is not only superior in offline rendering, but also outperforms traditional Path Tracing methods in real-time rendering settings, such as interactive applications and games.

</details>


### [261] [Texture Independently Drives Liking in AI-Generated Alternative Protein Burgers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08365)
*Vahidullah Tac,Aeneas O. Koosis,Ellen Kuhl*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究结合101名参与者的盲测感官数据与机械质地剖面分析，比较了AI生成的五种汉堡与动物基、植物基、蘑菇基、混合肉饼及经典巨无霸汉堡。主要发现：动物基汉堡具有独特的感官-机械区域；蘑菇基和植物基汉堡以蛋白质依赖性方式偏离该区域；回弹性是感知肉味和质地的最强机械相关量；质地与风味独立预测总体喜好度，其中肉味是质地喜好的主导预测因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纹理影响我们对食物的感知和喜好，但机械测量与感官纹理感知之间的明确关联仍然难以捉摸，本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 结合101名参与者的盲测感官数据与机械质地剖面分析（TPA），比较六种汉堡（包含AI生成、动物基、植物基、蘑菇基、混合及巨无霸）的纹理特征。

Result: 动物基汉堡占据独特的感官-机械区域；蘑菇基（偏弹性和胶粘）和植物基（偏干、脆、易碎）以蛋白质依赖性方式偏离；混合汉堡保持与动物基相当的感官特征；回弹性是感知肉味和纹理的最强机械相关量；质地与风味独立预测总体喜好，肉味是质地喜好的主导预测因子。

Conclusion: 回弹性被确定为质地工程的有希望靶点，质地应被视为可持续替代蛋白质的关键设计目标。

Abstract: Texture shapes how we perceive and like food, yet clear links between mechanical measurements and sensory perception of texture remain elusive. Here we combine sensory data from a blind tasting with 101 participants with mechanical texture profile analysis across six burgers to identify the textural features that drive consumer perception and liking. We compare five burgers -- generated with artificial intelligence -- with animal-based, plant-based, mushroom-based, and hybrid animal-mushroom patties, and the classical Big\,Mac. Three main findings emerge: First, animal-based burgers occupy a distinctive and coherent sensory-mechanical region associated with attributes such as firm, fatty, and holds together. Second, mushroom- and plant-based burgers deviate from this region in protein-dependent ways: mushroom-based burgers associate with springy and gummy textures, while plant-based burgers associate with dry, brittle, and crumbly textures. Hybrid animal-mushroom burgers, however, maintain sensory profiles comparable to fully animal-based burgers. Third, resilience emerges as the strongest mechanical correlate of perceived meatiness and sensory texture, while stiffness and hardness show no statistically significant association with consumer perception. Texture independently predicts overall liking alongside flavor: increasing texture liking by one point increases overall liking by 0.28. Among all sensory attributes, meatiness is the dominant predictor of texture liking. These findings identify resilience as a promising target for texture engineering and establish texture as a critical design objective for sustainable alternative proteins.

</details>


### [262] [Pushing Biomolecular Utility-Diversity Frontiers with Supergroup Relative Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08659)
*Xinwu Ye,He Cao,Hao Li,Bin Feng,Zijing Liu,Xiangru Tang,Yu Li,Shenghua Gao*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出SGRPO框架，通过集合级多样性直接构建奖励信号，在分子和蛋白质设计中实现了效用与多样性的帕累托最优前沿扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生物分子生成器使用奖励反馈优化任务效用，但追求纯效用会导致生成样本集中于狭窄的候选族，而维持多样性困难因为样本多样性是集合级属性。

Method: 提出Supergroup Relative Policy Optimization (SGRPO)，对每个条件采样超组候选集，比较同一条件下的多样性，通过留一法多样性贡献将集合级多样性奖励重新分配给单个 rollout，再与 rollout 级效用结合。框架与具体生成器、效用奖励或多样性度量解耦，可配合不同GRPO风格方法。

Result: 在从头小分子设计、口袋基小分子设计和从头蛋白质设计任务上，SGRPO扩展了效用-多样性帕累托前沿，取得最佳前沿级指标；集合级多样性奖励在小群体下仍有效，有助于保持生成分布覆盖。

Conclusion: SGRPO通过直接优化集合级多样性，有效缓解了奖励驱动生成中的多样性坍缩问题，为生物分子生成的后训练提供了通用解决方案。

Abstract: Biomolecular generators are often adapted with reward feedback to improve task-specific utility, but pushing utility alone can concentrate generation on a narrow family of candidates. Maintaining diversity is difficult because sample diversity is a set-level property. We introduce Supergroup Relative Policy Optimization (SGRPO), a flexible GRPO-style framework that directly constructs rewards from set-level diversity. For each condition, SGRPO samples a supergroup of candidate sets, compares their diversity under the same condition, and redistributes the group diversity reward to individual rollouts through leave-one-out diversity contributions before combining it with rollout-level utility. This design decouples SGRPO from a particular generator, utility reward, or diversity metric, and allows instantiation with different GRPO-style approaches. We evaluate SGRPO on de novo small-molecule design, pocket-based small-molecule design, and de novo protein design, instantiating it with both GRPO and Coupled-GRPO across autoregressive and discrete diffusion generators. Across decoding sweeps, SGRPO expands the utility-diversity Pareto frontier and achieves the best frontier-level metrics relative to pretrained generators, GRPO, and memory-assisted GRPO when applicable. Our analyses further show that direct set-level diversity rewards remain effective with small groups and help preserve broader generation-distribution coverage during post-training. The code is available at https://github.com/IDEA-XL/SGRPO.

</details>


### [263] [An Overlapping Schwarz Space-Time Refinement Framework for Material Point Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09097)
*Zhaofeng Luo,Minchen Li,Yupeng Jiang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于物质点法的重叠Schwarz时空细化框架(OS-MPM)，通过粗-细子域重叠耦合与Schwarz迭代实现局部时空细化，在保证精度的同时最高可降低9.15倍计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决物质点法(MPM)在强局部变形、接触和大几何非线性问题中计算效率低下的问题，现有细化策略依赖于修改基函数、过渡核或强制界面约束，破坏了标准MPM的模块化结构。

Method: 将计算域分解为具有异质时空分辨率的重叠粗、细子域，各子域保持标准MPM离散；通过基于质量加权的空间传输与时间插值的MPM特定Schwarz迭代实现子循环耦合；将耦合复杂性转移至非匹配网格界面算子。

Result: 在重力驱动悬臂梁、赫兹接触和弹性夹杂物等算例中准确再现了解析解或细网格参考解；夹杂物基准问题中，在最优分辨率下误差与单域细模拟相当或略低，计算成本最高降低9.15倍；三维折叠算例验证了方法的普适性。

Conclusion: 该方法为MPM提供了一种精确、模块化且高效的局部时空细化途径。

Abstract: We propose an overlapping Schwarz space-time refinement framework for the material point method (OS-MPM) to improve computational efficiency in problems with strongly localized deformation, contact, and large geometric nonlinearity. The method decomposes the domain into overlapping coarse and fine subdomains with heterogeneous spatial and temporal resolutions, while retaining standard MPM discretizations within each subdomain. Coarse-fine coupling is achieved through an MPM-specific Schwarz iteration combining mass-weighted spatial transmission and temporal interpolation for sub-cycling. In contrast to refinement strategies based on modified basis functions, transition kernels, or strongly enforced interface constraints, the proposed approach preserves the modular structure of standard MPM and shifts the coupling complexity to nonmatching-grid interface operators within the Schwarz alternating procedure. Numerical examples, including a gravity-driven cantilever beam, Hertzian contact, and an elastic inclusion problem, show that the method reproduces analytical or fine-resolution reference solutions with good accuracy and convergence behavior. In the inclusion benchmark, the proposed framework achieves comparable or slightly lower error than single-domain fine simulations at the finest tested resolutions, while reducing computational cost by up to 9.15 times. A three-dimensional folding example further demonstrates the generality of the framework. These results indicate that the proposed method provides an accurate, modular, and efficient route for local space-time refinement in MPM.

</details>


### [264] [Score-Based Generative Modeling through Anisotropic Stochastic Partial Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08976)
*Sascha Holl,Jente Vandersanden,Gurprit Singh,Hans-Peter Seidel*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一类各向异性随机偏微分方程（SPDE）替代传统SDE扩散过程，通过在正向过程中保留数据几何结构更长时间，提升生成图像质量，在无条件生成和条件生成任务上均优于SDE基线和Flow Matching方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于SDE的扩散模型在正向过程中逐步破坏所有图像信息，导致几何结构过早丢失，限制了生成保真度。作者希望设计一种保留数据几何结构更长时间的扩散过程，使反向生成能利用残余几何线索，从而提升重建质量。

Method: 提出一类各向异性SPDE，包含两个关键组件：1) 漂移项，通过结构平滑实现确定性的方向依赖信息破坏；2) 扩散系数，通过噪声注入实现随机破坏。两者均由各向异性系数控制，实现方向依赖的可控信息退化，从而在更长时间尺度上保留数据的几何结构。

Result: 在无条件图像生成任务中，各向异性扩散在像素空间和潜空间实验上均优于基于SDE的基线和当前最先进的Flow Matching方法。在条件式笔画到图像生成任务中也验证了各向异性的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的各向异性SPDE框架为生成建模提供了新的理论基础，通过保留几何结构更长时间来提升生成质量，有望替代传统各向同性扩散过程。

Abstract: Score-based generative modeling (SBGM) has achieved state-of-the-art performance in image generation, with the quality of generated images being highly dependent on the design of the forward (diffusion) process. Among these, models based on stochastic differential equations (SDEs) have proven particularly effective. While traditional methods aim to progressively destroy all image information to enable reconstruction from pure noise, we propose a class of anisotropic stochastic partial differential equations (SPDEs) that preserve the geometric structure of the data over longer time scales throughout the transformation. These SPDEs consist of a drift term that enforces deterministic destruction via structured smoothing, and a diffusion coefficient that enables random destruction through noise injection. Both components are governed by anisotropy coefficients, enabling controlled, direction-dependent information degradation. This framework provides the theoretical foundation for a novel anisotropic score-based generative model. By retaining geometric structure for longer time scales, the backward generative process can exploit residual geometric cues, leading to improved reconstruction fidelity. We empirically validate this improvement in a proof-of-concept implementation on unconditional image generation, showing that anisotropic diffusion can achieve superior image quality metrics. We demonstrate consistent improvements in both pixel and latent space experiments over the SDE-driven baseline as well as over the state-of-the-art Flow Matching approach. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of the introduced anisotropy in a conditional stroke-to-image generation task.

</details>


### [265] [Rao-Blackwellized Markov chain Monte Carlo Light Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09117)
*Sascha Holl,Gurprit Singh,Hans-Peter Seidel*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文针对光传输模拟中马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛方法的方差问题，提出了一种新型Rao-Blackwellization（RB）技术，该技术计算高效且能显著降低方差，在Metropolis-Hastings和Jump Restore算法中均优于传统的waste-recycling方法，并通过大量实验验证了其性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光传输模拟中，传统waste-recycling的Rao-Blackwellization方法在实际应用中方差降低效果甚微，缺乏有效的方差缩减手段。

Method: 提出一种针对通用Metropolis-Hastings算法的新型RB技术，并将其适配到Jump Restore算法中，实现计算高效且显著的方差降低。

Result: 在等时间和等样本数量比较下，新RB技术在方差降低和收敛速度两方面均持续优于waste-recycling方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的RB技术可替代传统waste-recycling，显著提升MH系列和Jump Restore光传输算法的性能。

Abstract: In light transport simulation, Markov chain Monte Carlo methods are particularly effective at exploring regions with complex lighting characteristics. However, estimator variance is a central concern across Monte Carlo methods in general. In light transport, high variance directly manifests as increased noise or, equivalently, longer rendering times at fixed image quality. Variance reduction techniques based on Rao-Blackwellization have proven particularly effective. In practice, however, the RB approach traditionally used in light transport, waste-recycling, can yield little to no measurable variance reduction, a fact we empirically confirm in this work. Motivated by this lack of effective variance reduction, we introduce a novel RB technique for the general-purpose Metropolis-Hastings algorithm that is computationally efficient and achieves substantial variance reduction. We show that this method consistently outperforms waste-recycling in terms of both variance reduction and convergence speed. Building on this result, we adapt the proposed RB approach to the recently introduced general-purpose Jump Restore algorithm, where it similarly achieves substantial variance reduction and accelerated convergence. Through extensive experiments in light transport simulation, we demonstrate that our \gls{rb} technique significantly outperforms the traditional approaches for both MH-based light transport algorithms and Jump Restore Light Transport, under both equal-time and equal-sample-count comparisons.

</details>

Result: 在比特币交易数据上，AutoRedTrader达到69.00%的错误信息曝光率和26.67%的攻击成功率，优于通用错误信息和红队测试基线；消融实验验证了所有模块对生成可检索且影响决策的金融错误信息的贡献。

Conclusion: AutoRedTrader能够有效评估微妙错误信息对金融智能体的影响，且历史市场证据有助于稳定智能体在误导性文本信号下的决策，为金融AI系统的安全性和鲁棒性提供了系统性的评估工具。

Abstract: LLM-based financial agents increasingly rely on both numerical market data and textual signals for sequential trading and stock prediction. However, financial misinformation often appears as subtle textual perturbations rather than explicit falsehoods, making it difficult to detect while still capable of significantly altering agent reasoning and decisions. To study this risk, we propose AutoRedTrader, an autonomous red-teaming framework that generates finance-specific misinformation through behavioral bias manipulation, minor textual perturbations, and rewriting strategies, with agent feedback used to strengthen attacks over time. We evaluate AutoRedTrader in a POMDP-based financial agent simulation environment, and further examine a time-series-informed grounding setting for robustness analysis. The framework enables systematic evaluation of how subtle misinformation affects financial agents and whether historical market evidence can stabilize decisions under misleading textual signals. We evaluate the framework on Bitcoin transaction data. The results show that AutoRedTrader achieves the strongest attack performance with 69.00% misinformation exposure rate and 26.67% attack success rate, outperforming general-purpose misinformation and red-teaming baselines. Ablation studies further show that all modules contribute to generating retrievable and decision-effective financial misinformation.

Human-in-the-loop is critical for resolving ambiguities and handling SPH-specific configurations. ### [268] [Evaluating Transit Accessibility to Education and Effects of Operational Delays in Japanese Regional Cities: A Case Study of Matsumoto City](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09467)
*Itsuki Sato,Kiyoshi Takami,Giancarlos Parady*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文利用日本松本市的实际GTFS数据，评估了频繁延误对高中通勤可达性的影响。研究发现，在允许步行、骑行至车站和公共交通组合出行的情况下，78%的15岁以下儿童可在90分钟往返内到达至少一所高中；延误的影响在连接市中心与郊区的公交线路上尤为显著，但某些区域因延误导致的换乘变化反而改善了可达性。研究提出了调整上学时间、公交优先等短期措施及将可达性纳入学校合并决策等长期策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用GTFS数据（包含计划时刻表和实际运营数据），评估松本市高中可达性；通过比较五天工作周的实际延误测量进行对比分析，并开展出行时间阈值的敏感性分析。

Result: 78%的儿童可在90分钟往返内到达至少一所高中，67%可在60分钟内到达；阈值延至120分钟可达市中心几乎所有学校，但总体比例仅增至81%。延误影响在郊区公交线路上最显著，但部分区域因不规则换乘和等待时间减少反而提升了可达性。

Conclusion: 研究强调需采取短期措施（调整上学时间、公交优先、增设校车路线）和长期策略（将公共交通可达性纳入学校合并决策），以确保不依赖私家车的教育机会公平。

Abstract: Realistic assessments of school commuting accessibility in areas with infrequent public transport services require accounting for operational delays; however, the impact of these delays has not been sufficiently examined. This study evaluates high-school accessibility in Matsumoto City, a regional city in Japan, using GTFS data representing both scheduled timetables and actual operating conditions. Accessibility levels are assessed under scheduled operations, while the effects of delays are examined through a comparative analysis based on actual delay measurements over a five-day workweek. Furthermore, a sensitivity analysis of travel-time thresholds was conducted. Results show that, when walking, cycling to stations, and public transport use are allowed, 78% of children under 15 can reach at least one high school within a 90-minute round trip, and 67% within a 60-minute round trip. Extending the threshold to 120 minutes enables access to nearly all schools in the city center, but the overall proportion increases only marginally to 81%. Delay impacts are particularly pronounced along bus routes connecting the central station with suburban areas, while in some areas, delays generate idiosyncratic events, where irregular transfers and reduced waiting times result in improved accessibility. Results underscore the need for both short-term measures,such as adjusting school start times, prioritizing buses, and introducing dedicated school routes, and long-term strategies, such as incorporating public transport accessibility into school consolidation decisions, to guarantee fair access to education opportunities without relying on private vehicles.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在广泛的实验中，QuantWeather展现出更优的概率预报技巧，同时大幅降低了推理时的计算和存储成本。

Abstract: Subseasonal precipitation forecasting is inherently uncertain due to chaotic atmospheric dynamics, making reliable uncertainty estimation essential for real-world applications. Existing approaches typically represent uncertainty through ensemble forecasts rather than directly modeling predictive distributions. However, due to systematic model biases, raw ensemble outputs are often not well calibrated and cannot be directly interpreted as reliable uncertainty estimates. As a result, operational systems rely on post-hoc calibration based on reforecast datasets, which are computationally expensive to generate and maintain. To address these limitations, we propose QuantWeather, an end-to-end probabilistic forecasting framework with a dual-head design. The probabilistic and deterministic heads are supervised with separate objectives and optimized jointly. The framework further supports stochastic sampling, enabling probabilistic outputs even with a single stochastic forward pass and allowing optional multi-sample aggregation. Extensive experiments show that QuantWeather demonstrates superior probabilistic forecasting skill while substantially reducing inference-time computational and storage costs.

### [270] [A Performance-Portable, Massively Parallel Distributed Nonuniform FFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10678)
*Paul Fischill,Andreas Adelmann,Sriramkrishnan Muralikrishnan*

TL;DR: 提出了首个面向异构超级计算机的分布式、性能可移植的非均匀快速傅里叶变换（NUFFT）实现，基于Kokkos框架，支持NVIDIA和AMD GPU，在Alps、JUWELS Booster和LUMI上实现了多达1024个GPU的扩展，并应用于大规模粒子-傅里叶等离子体模拟。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NUFFT实现仅限于共享内存执行，问题规模受限于单节点内存，无法利用分布式异构超级计算机的计算资源处理更大规模的问题。

Method: 基于Kokkos框架开发了分布式、性能可移植的NUFFT实现，设计了针对不同精度要求和架构优化的多种扩展和插值核函数，支持NVIDIA和AMD GPU，无需修改代码即可运行。

Result: 在单GPU吞吐量上匹配或超越了cuFINUFFT；在Alps (NVIDIA GH200)、JUWELS Booster (NVIDIA A100)和LUMI (AMD MI250X)上实现高达1024个GPU的强扩展；成功应用于包含1024^3个傅里叶模式和86亿粒子的Landau阻尼等离子体模拟。

Abstract: The nonuniform fast Fourier transform (NUFFT) enables spectral methods for problems with irregularly spaced samples, with applications in medical imaging, molecular dynamics, and kinetic plasma simulations. Existing implementations are limited to shared-memory execution, restricting problem sizes to what fits on a single node. We present the first distributed, performance-portable NUFFT for heterogeneous supercomputers. Our Kokkos-based implementation runs without modification on NVIDIA and AMD GPUs. We develop multiple spreading and interpolation kernels optimized for different accuracy requirements and architectures. Our spreading kernels match or exceed the single-GPU throughput of the state-of-the-art CUDA-based NUFFT library cuFINUFFT at production particle densities, while our Kokkos-based implementation additionally supports AMD GPUs. Strong scaling experiments on Alps (NVIDIA GH200), JUWELS Booster (NVIDIA A100), and LUMI (AMD MI250X) demonstrate scaling up to 1024 GPUs. At scale, the distributed FFT is a significant part of the total runtime, making higher NUFFT accuracy less expensive. We apply the method to massively parallel Particle-in-Fourier simulations of Landau damping with up to $1024^3$ Fourier modes and 8.6 billion particles on Alps, JUWELS, and LUMI, demonstrating that distributed NUFFTs enable kinetic plasma simulations at resolutions previously inaccessible to spectral particle methods.

### [271] [On Distributed Parallelization Strategies for Particle-in-Fourier Schemes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10729)
*Sriramkrishnan Muralikrishnan,Paul Fischill,Andreas Adelmann,Robert Speck*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出并比较了用于等离子体动力学模拟的粒子-傅里叶(PIF)方案的三种分布式并行化策略：区域分解、粒子分解和时空分解，并在超级计算机上进行了基准测试和性能分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对粒子-傅里叶(PIF)方案在动力学等离子体模拟中缺乏系统并行化策略比较的问题，探索不同分解策略的适用场景与性能特征。

Method: 提出了三种并行化策略：1) 区域分解——粒子和傅里叶模式均在MPI ranks间分割；2) 粒子分解——仅粒子分割，每个rank拥有所有模式；3) 时空分解——基于parareal算法在粒子分解基础上增加时间并行化。在开源库IPPL中实现，使用3D-3V朗道阻尼和Penning阱基准问题在Alps和JUWELS booster超算上进行扩展性研究。

Result: 描述了各策略的通信模式、最佳参数区间及优劣势，分析了各策略中主导组件的时间消耗，识别了未来优化方向。

Conclusion: 三种并行化策略各有适用场景：区域分解适合模式数较少的情况，粒子分解适合粒子数远大于模式数的场景，时空分解在特定条件下可提供额外加速。研究为PIF方案的高效并行实现提供了指导，并指出了进一步优化的潜在方向。

Abstract: We present and compare distributed parallelization strategies for the particle-in-Fourier (PIF) schemes used in kinetic plasma simulations. The different strategies are i) domain decomposition, where both the particles and Fourier modes are split between the MPI ranks ii) particle decomposition, where only the particles are split between the ranks and each rank carries all the modes, and, iii) space-time decomposition, in which time parallelization based on the parareal algorithm is added on top of the particle decomposition. We describe the different communication patterns involved in each of the strategies, the parameter regimes where they work best, and explain their advantages and disadvantages. We implement the strategies within the open-source, performance portable library IPPL and conduct scaling studies with 3D-3V Landau damping and Penning trap benchmark problems on Alps and JUWELS booster supercomputers. We analyze the dominant component timings in each of the strategies and identify areas for future optimizations.

</details>

*Zijun Zhan,Yaxian Dong,Daniel Mawunyo Doe,Yuqing Hu,Shaohua Cao,Zhu Han*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI-RAN是支撑边缘AI生态的关键架构，需要良好的激励机制确保可持续发展。然而现有激励设计面临两大挑战：1) 信息不对称——运营商仅部分了解AI用户的效用函数；2) 多运营商竞争——现实中多个运营商共存，混乱的对抗性竞争可能损害运营商效用。

Method: 1) 扩展静态匹配与合约模型，联合刻画多竞争运营商的合约设计、用户-运营商匹配及市场状态动态演化；2) 每个运营商的激励采用合约菜单形式，每个合约项包含AI服务延迟协议及对应价格；3) 将AI服务过程建模为三个独立队列，利用排队论和Chernoff界刻画延迟协议违反概率；4) 提出混合稳定匹配与合约算法，联合更新用户侧匹配决策和运营商侧合约菜单。

Result: 在面向远程操作的AIGC服务仿真中，所提方法相比基准方案，在代表性设置下将AI-RAN运营商总效用提升至少56.8%。

Conclusion: 所提出的匹配与合约激励框架在信息不对称和竞争环境下具有有效性和鲁棒性，能够显著提升运营商效用，促进AI-RAN生态的可持续发展。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence radio access networks (AI-RANs) are a promising architecture for bolstering the prosperity of the edge AI ecosystem. A well-designed incentive mechanism can further ensure the sustainable development of this ecosystem. However, incentive mechanism design faces two major challenges: 1) information asymmetry, where AI-RAN operators have only partial knowledge of AI users' utility functions, and 2) competition, as multiple AI-RAN operators coexist in real-world markets. Remarkably, chaotic and adversarial competition might compromise AI-RAN operators' utility. To this end, we develop a matching-with-contracts framework for incentive mechanism design in AI-RAN service markets. The framework extends the static matching-with-contracts model by jointly characterizing the contract design of multiple competitive operators, user-operator matching, and dynamic evolution of the market state. Specifically, the incentive mechanism offered by each AI-RAN operator takes the form of a contract menu, where each contract item consists of an AI service latency agreement and a corresponding price. We model the AI service process as three independent queues and characterize the violation probability of the latency agreement using queueing theory and the Chernoff bound. To derive an effective incentive mechanism, we further propose a mixed stable matching-with-contracts algorithm that jointly updates user-side matching decisions and operator-side contract menus. Simulation results for a teleoperation-oriented AIGC service demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed method. Compared with benchmark schemes, our method improves the total utility of AI-RAN operators by at least 56.8\% under representative settings.

</details>
